scroll-mt-20"><div class="bg-card/30 border-x border-b px-6 py-8 sm:px-8 sm:py-12 lg:px-12 lg:py-16"><div class="container max-w-3xl"><h2 class="mb-6 text-center text-3xl font-bold">Frequently Asked Questions</h2><div class="mb-8"><div class="grid grid-cols-1 gap-2"><div class="bg-card border"><div class="flex items-center justify-between px-6 py-4"><h5 class="flex-1 cursor-pointer text-base font-medium leading-tight">What is a Next.js SaaS starter kit?</h5><button class="text-primary size-8"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-chevron-down size-4" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m6 9 6 6 6-6"></path></svg></button></div><div class="text-foreground/60 -mt-2 p-6 pt-0 hidden">A SaaS starter kit is a codebase based on the framework of your choice that includes all the common functionality and tools you need to build a Saas / web app. It helps you to get started quickly and saves you a lot of time and headache when building a SaaS application.</div></div><div class="bg-card border"><div class="flex items-center justify-between px-6 py-4"><h5 class="flex-1 cursor-pointer text-base font-medium leading-tight">What is the difference between a Next.js starter kit, a Next.js boilerplate and a Next.js starter template?</h5><button class="text-primary size-8"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-chevron-down size-4" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m6 9 6 6 6-6"></path></svg></button></div><div class="text-foreground/60 -mt-2 p-6 pt-0 hidden">The terms "starter kit", "boilerplate" and "template" are often used interchangeably. In the context of supastarter, we use the term "starter kit" because it includes a lot more than just the boilerplate code like the extensive documentation, our community of 950+ members, a discord server, a blog with tutorials and guides, a dedicated support channel and more.</div></div><div class="bg-card border"><div class="flex items-center justify-between px-6 py-4"><h5 class="flex-1 cursor-pointer text-base font-medium leading-tight">How is supastarter different from other starter kits or boilerplates?</h5><button class="text-primary size-8"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-chevron-down size-4" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m6 9 6 6 6-6"></path></svg></button></div><div class="text-foreground/60 -mt-2 p-6 pt-0 hidden"><div>supastarter is a full-featured starter kit that includes all the common functionality and tools you need to build a SaaS app. Compared to other starter kits, supastarter is not only meant for building fast MVPs, but giving you a starting point that enables you to build a production-ready and scalable SaaS. It is built with the following core pricinples:<ul class="mt-4 space-y-3"><li><strong>Modular:</strong> supastarter is built with a modular architecture that allows you to easily add or remove features.</li><li><strong>Scalable:</strong> supastarter is built with scalability in mind. It uses a serverless architecture to ensure your app can scale with your business.</li><li><strong>Production-ready:</strong> supastarter includes all the common functionality and tools you need to build a SaaS app. It is built with best practices in mind and is fully type-safe.</li><li><strong>Customizable:</strong> supastarter is fully customizable. You can easily add your own features, change the design, or integrate with other services.</li></ul></div></div></div><div class="bg-card border"><div class="flex items-center justify-between px-6 py-4"><h5 class="flex-1 cursor-pointer text-base font-medium leading-tight">How do I get access to the boilerplate code?</h5><button class="text-primary size-8"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-chevron-down size-4" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m6 9 6 6 6-6"></path></svg></button></div><div class="text-foreground/60 -mt-2 p-6 pt-0 hidden">Immedietly after your purchase you will receive a link with which you can add your github account to the private supastarter github repository. From there you can clone the starter template and start building your SaaS.</div></div><div class="bg-card border"><div class="flex items-center justify-between px-6 py-4"><h5 class="flex-1 cursor-pointer text-base font-medium leading-tight">Is the codebase being maintained regularly?</h5><button class="text-primary size-8"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-chevron-down size-4" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m6 9 6 6 6-6"></path></svg></button></div><div class="text-foreground/60 -mt-2 p-6 pt-0 hidden">Of course. Since we use this project for our own client projects, we make sure all the packages are up-to-date and everything is working fine.</div></div><div class="bg-card border"><div class="flex items-center justify-between px-6 py-4"><h5 class="flex-1 cursor-pointer text-base font-medium leading-tight">What if I find a bug?</h5><button class="text-primary size-8"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-chevron-down size-4" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m6 9 6 6 6-6"></path></svg></button></div><div class="text-foreground/60 -mt-2 p-6 pt-0 hidden">Once you have access to the supastarter repository you will be able to create issues for bugs which we will fix as soon as possible. You will also have access to the discord server where you can ask questions and get help from us and the community.</div></div><div class="bg-card border"><div class="flex items-center justify-between px-6 py-4"><h5 class="flex-1 cursor-pointer text-base font-medium leading-tight">What do I get for my money?</h5><button class="text-primary size-8"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-chevron-down size-4" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m6 9 6 6 6-6"></path></svg></button></div><div class="text-foreground/60 -mt-2 p-6 pt-0 hidden">supastarter is a one-time-purchase that will give you lifetime access to the github repository with the code. It also means you get free updates and support in our discord channel.</div></div><div class="bg-card border"><div class="flex items-center justify-between px-6 py-4"><h5 class="flex-1 cursor-pointer text-base font-medium leading-tight">What am I allowed to do with the Next.js starter template?</h5><button class="text-primary size-8"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-chevron-down size-4" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m6 9 6 6 6-6"></path></svg></button></div><div class="text-foreground/60 -mt-2 p-6 pt-0 hidden">You are allowed to build unlimited projects with it (commercial projects too). You are not allowed to resell the code or parts of it. You are also not allowed to publish the code or parts of it as a template or boilerplate. See the <a class="text-secondary" href="/legal/license">license page</a> for more details.</div></div><div class="bg-card border"><div class="flex items-center justify-between px-6 py-4"><h5 class="flex-1 cursor-pointer text-base font-medium leading-tight">Can I see what I am getting before purchasing?</h5><button class="text-primary size-8"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-chevron-down size-4" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m6 9 6 6 6-6"></path></svg></button></div><div class="text-foreground/60 -mt-2 p-6 pt-0 hidden">Sure. You can <a href="https://demo.supastarter.dev" class="text-secondary" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer">try the demo</a> to experience all the features yourself or check out the <a class="text-secondary" href="/docs">documentation</a>. If you have any other questions, contact us on twitter @supastarter or via email at contact@supastarter.dev.</div></div><div class="bg-card border"><div class="flex items-center justify-between px-6 py-4"><h5 class="flex-1 cursor-pointer text-base font-medium leading-tight">Do I get access to only one framework or all of them?</h5><button class="text-primary size-8"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-chevron-down size-4" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m6 9 6 6 6-6"></path></svg></button></div><div class="text-foreground/60 -mt-2 p-6 pt-0 hidden">When you purchase access to the starter kit, you always only purchase one framework version. If you want to purchase access the other versions, you can do so separately.</div></div><div class="bg-card border"><div class="flex items-center justify-between px-6 py-4"><h5 class="flex-1 cursor-pointer text-base font-medium leading-tight">Can supastarter be used to build an AI SaaS?</h5><button class="text-primary size-8"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-chevron-down size-4" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m6 9 6 6 6-6"></path></svg></button></div><div class="text-foreground/60 -mt-2 p-6 pt-0 hidden">Yes, supastarter can be used to build an AI SaaS. We acutally have built-in support for the Vercel AI SDK which supports all major LLMs and we have guides on how to integrate it with your project.</div></div><div class="bg-card border"><div class="flex items-center justify-between px-6 py-4"><h5 class="flex-1 cursor-pointer text-base font-medium leading-tight">Can I download the documentation for offline use or for AI coding agents?</h5><button class="text-primary size-8"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-chevron-down size-4" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m6 9 6 6 6-6"></path></svg></button></div><div class="text-foreground/60 -mt-2 p-6 pt-0 hidden">Yes, the latest version of the documentation is at any time available for download.<br><a href="https://supastarter.dev/nextjs-docs.zip" class="text-secondary" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer">Next.js Documentation</a> - <a href="https://supastarter.dev/nuxt-docs.zip" class="text-secondary" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer">Nuxt Documentation</a></div></div></div></div><div class="border-border border p-6 text-center"><p class="text-foreground mb-2 font-medium">Still have questions about whether supastarter is right for you?</p><p class="text-foreground/60 mb-4 text-sm">Get a personalized fit check based on your project and skill level.</p><div class="flex justify-center"><button class="inline-flex items-center justify-center font-semibold tracking-wide transition-all duration-150 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-offset-2 focus-visible:ring-offset-background focus-visible:ring-ring disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 bg-primary/10 text-primary hover:bg-primary/15 h-8 rounded-full px-3 text-xs"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-list-checks mr-2 size-5" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m3 17 2 2 4-4"></path><path d="m3 7 2 2 4-4"></path><path d="M13 6h8"></path><path d="M13 12h8"></path><path d="M13 18h8"></path></svg>Check if supastarter fits your project</button></div></div></div></div></section><section id="about" class="container relative"><div class="border-x border-b px-6 py-8 sm:px-8 sm:py-12 lg:px-12 lg:py-16"><div class="flex flex-col items-center gap-8 lg:flex-row"><div class="text-center lg:text-left"><h2 class="text-foreground text-balance text-3xl font-bold lg:text-4xl">Our mission for supastarter</h2><div class="mt-4 text-base"><p class="text-foreground/60">We are building supastarter to help indie hackers and developers to build their SaaS with a solid stack in record time.
